## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task models population growth rate dP/dt as a function of population P and time t, which is the fundamental setup of ODE-based population dynamics models. The presence of both t and P suggests either a non-autonomous model (time-varying parameters) or a more complex growth law.

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Exponential growth: dP_dt = c0 * P (unlimited growth, Malthusian model)
- Logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) (density-dependent growth with carrying capacity)
- Gompertz growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P) (asymmetric sigmoidal growth)
- Theta-logistic: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (generalized logistic with shape parameter)
- Allee effect (strong): dP_dt = c0 * P * (P - c1) * (1 - c2 * P) (growth with minimum viable population)
- Allee effect (weak): dP_dt = c0 * P * P * (1 - c1 * P) (quadratic density dependence at low P)
- Beverton-Holt continuous: dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (saturating per-capita growth)
- Seasonal logistic: dP_dt = c0 * (1 + c1 * sin(c2 * t)) * P * (1 - c3 * P) (periodically forced logistic)
- Time-varying exponential: dP_dt = c0 * P * exp(c1 * t) (time-dependent growth rate)
- Logistic with harvesting: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 * P (logistic with proportional removal)
- Richards growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) * c3 (flexible asymmetric growth curve)
- Polynomial per-capita rate: dP_dt = P * (c0 + c1 * P + c2 * P**2) (cubic population dynamics)
- Seasonal Gompertz: dP_dt = c0 * P * (c1 - log(P)) * (1 + c2 * sin(c3 * t)) (Gompertz with periodic forcing)
- Delayed density dependence proxy: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) + c2 * t * P (linear trend in growth)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Density dependence → multiplicative factor (1 - c*P) or (1 - (c*P)**n) representing resource limitation as population approaches carrying capacity
- Allee effects → additional multiplicative factor (P - c) creating a critical threshold below which growth is negative
- Per-capita growth rate structure → dP/dt typically factored as P * f(P,t), where f represents per-capita growth rate
- Seasonal/periodic forcing → multiplicative modulation by (1 + c*sin(c*t)) or (1 + c*cos(c*t)) on growth rate parameters
- Multiple equilibria in population models → polynomial expressions in P (cubic or higher) allowing for multiple roots where dP/dt = 0
- Logarithmic density dependence → log(P) terms appear in Gompertz-type models where growth slows logarithmically near carrying capacity
- Cooperative growth at low density → P**2 or higher power terms dominating at small P, reflecting mate-finding or group benefits
- Rational per-capita rate → division by (1 + c*P) representing saturating effects of competition or resource depletion
